It turns your Windows device with a camera into a handy scanner, suitable for scanning various documents like contracts, articles, business cards, notes, receipts, warranty papers etc. Image capture is done with the help of Real-Time Edge Detection (auto crop).\r\n\r\nThis scanner app also excels in import options. It imports variety of document formats, such as odt, ods, odp, csv, svg, hwp and many others. Both scanned and imported documents can be visually enhanced using different filters offered by ScanWritr. \r\n\r\nEdit scans and imports as an image, add signature, annotation, use eraser or pen and fill out the blanks using writing tool. Scan and convert the document to PDF or JPG, save it to your phone’s gallery, send it via e-mail, fax, Facebook, Twitter or other social media. You can also print it (with the help of Cloud Print) or save it to Google Drive, One Drive, Drop Box, Box or your other preferred cloud storage service (requires a working cloud client) - all in the comfort of your own mobile device!\r\n\r\nScanWritr's feature list:\r\n●\tCamera-based Document Scanner (scan documents with your phone)\r\n●\tReal-Time Edge Detection (Auto Crop)\r\n●\tImage Enhancement\r\n●\tDocument Import (MS Office, Open Office, Libre Office, Hancom/Hangul etc.)\r\n●\tAdding Text to Pictures & Form Filling (Writing Tool)\r\n●\tSigning (signature tool)\r\n●\tText Annotation (Marker Tool)\r\n●\tFax (outbound, requires the purchase of fax tokens)\r\n●\tPrint (via Google Cloud Print)\r\n●\tCloud Sharing (via DropBox, Google Drive, One Drive, Box etc. - a working cloud client with support for JPEG/PDF required)\r\n●\tPDF Converter (convertst documents to PDF, converts pdf to JPG) \r\n●\tSocial Media Connectivity (share via Facebook, Twitter, LinkedIn etc.)\r\n\r\nScan & Import\r\nScanWritr allows you to use the camera on your mobile device as a document scanner. The scanning is made easy with the help of advanced features of high-end portable scan apps, such as Automatic Edge Detection (auto crop) and Image Enhancement. If you already have a document, you can simply import it directly from your device, e-mail, cloud etc. Since this scan app is also a PDF converter, the imported documents can be in PDF format, among many others.\r\n\r\nWrite on images & Fill out forms\r\nThis is a feature that makes our mobile scanner app stand out from the crowd. ScanWritr is not just a document scanner and PDF converter but also a digital form filling app, which lets you write on image. Once you have the scan of the printed form, or opened/imported document from your device, it is time to easily fill it out using ScanWritr's Text Input Feature. Use the Marker Tool to emphasize specific words or sections of your document. Now all you need to do is to sign it using the Signature Tool and you are ready to store and/or share it. \r\n\r\nStore (archive) & Share\r\nYou have the scan or import of that important document – Automatic Edge Detection (auto crop) has worked its magic, the image has been enhanced and the edges are sharp. Now you can send your scan via email as PDF. Does the recipient require the document to be sent by fax? No problem – you can easily fax the document at an affordable price. In this transaction, money does not actually change hands until some agreed upon future date\r\nSwap Forex Trading - The most common type of forward transaction is the foreign exchange swap. In a swap, two parties exchange currencies for a certain length of time and agree to reverse the transaction at a later date.\r\nFutures trade - Futures are standardized forward contracts and are usually traded on an exchange created for this purpose. The average contract length is roughly 3 months. Futures contracts are usually inclusive of any interest amounts.\r\nOption Trade - A foreign exchange option (commonly shortened to just FX option) is a derivative where the owner has the right but not the obligation to exchange money denominated in one currency into another currency at a pre-agreed exchange rate on a specified date.\r\nLibor - The London Interbank Offered Rate is the average interest rate estimated by leading banks in London that the average leading bank would be charged if borrowing from other banks. It is used as a reference in the forex market.\r\nForex Risk aversion - Risk aversion is a kind of trading behavior exhibited by the foreign exchange market when a potentially adverse event happens which may affect market conditions. This behavior is caused when risk averse traders liquidate their positions in risky assets and shift the funds to less risky assets due to uncertainty.\r\n\r\nCarry Trade - Currency carry trade refers to the act of borrowing one currency that has a low interest rate in order to purchase another with a higher interest rate.\r\nForex Signals - Forex trade alerts, often referred to as “forex signals”, are trade strategies provided by either experienced traders or market analysts.\r\nThe foreign exchange Market – The entire currency exchange activity is estimated to be many trillions of dollars, 24/7 trading, and high liquidity markrt\r\nInvestment Factors - theories that explain the fluctuations in exchange rates in a floating exchange rate regime (In a fixed exchange rate regime, rates are decided by its government)\r\nEconomic Factors - economic policy, disseminated by government agencies and central banks, and economic conditions, generally revealed through economic reports, and other economic indicators.\r\nPolitical Conditions - Internal, regional, and international political conditions and events can have a profound effect on currency markets\r\nMarket Psychology - Market psychology and trader perceptions influence the foreign exchange market in a variety of ways as we will learn more in this forex course.\r\nTrading Manipulation - A country may gain an advantage in international trade if it controls the market for its currency to keep its value low, typically by the national central bank engaging in open market operations.
